Local News Two

The Special District Court Heard the Wu Suzhong Case Yesterday 190

The Judge Advocates for Investigation of True Name

Result Pending Submission of Evidence for Further Verification

Shishi Xinbao reporter Wu Suzhong, accused of being the Communist Hu Yu, was detained by detectives on August 1 and brought to the Special District Court, ordered to be held in custody pending investigation. Yesterday morning, the trial date arrived again. The police brought Hu to the Special District Court. Presiding Judge Xu Jiawei stated that this case should be handled by the High Court, according to a previous ruling, he was bound and could not hear the case, so he transferred it to the Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court. Judge Ye Zaizhou, upon taking the stand in the First Tribunal, announced the reason for the High Court's lack of jurisdiction over the case, stating that it was a Communist case transferred from the interior, not a public case filed by the police. Therefore, the defendant was returned to the District Court, where Judge Xu began the trial in the First Tribunal. Prosecutor Xu Geng also attended to perform his duties, while the Songhu Garrison Headquarters specially sent legal counsel James Kee-Ong to the court. First, Detective Wang Bin from the Garrison Headquarters' Investigation Team stated the reason for transferring the defendant, saying that it was based on a secret agent named Xu, who, on May 29, while transferring another Communist case to the High Court Branch, saw the report in court. Xu immediately told him that this person was also an important member of the Communist Party. He then planned to arrest him, but police lawyer Ru Bao-yi told him that if the interior authorities wanted to arrest a suspect in the concession, they had to obtain an arrest warrant from the court, unless it was a case of flagrant offense. Therefore, he abandoned the plan. Later, he obtained an arrest warrant from the court and apprehended him on Nanjing Road on August 1. However, Xu has not returned to the team since leaving on August 3. Besides, although there are people who can testify that the defendant is indeed the Communist Hu Yu, they are unwilling to appear in court to testify. Next, lawyer Ru recounted the events of June 1, when Detective Wang wanted to arrest the defendant at the High Court Branch but was told that he could not arrest him without an arrest warrant. Then, detective Zhang Yi from the Old Gate Police Station reported the situation after arresting the defendant and being instructed to search the defendant's residence at No. 732, Qipu Road, saying that all the letters and other items found were in the name of Wu Suzhong, and submitted the documents and newspapers found. Then the debate began. First, the police lawyer, Mr. Bolland, translated, "According to Article 1, Section 2 of the National Revolutionary Army's Army Trial Regulations promulgated by the National Government on February 17, the Ordinary Court should try non-military personnel who have committed crimes. The defendant is a journalist, not an active-duty soldier. Even if he has violated military law, he is not subject to trial by military organs. According to the plaintiff, the defendant is a Communist, then he has committed crimes under Article 103 of the Criminal Law and the Anti-Revolutionary Punishment Law, all of which belong to ordinary law. Now, the requester for transfer is the Headquarters, but it does not belong to a military offender. The military organ has absolutely no right to hear the case. The ones who can transfer it are only the Shanghai District Court or the Jiangsu High Court. If it is transferred to a military organ, it should be forwarded by the Public Security Bureau, but there must be proof of the crime first. Article 6 of the signed agreement to recover the court specifies that a criminal found in the Public Concession, after investigation by the court of the various countries, can be transferred to the non-concession offices, but by the entrustment of other Chinese modern courts, if the court has confirmed the identity, it can be transferred immediately. Now, the plaintiff has not submitted conclusive evidence. Although Detective Wang has made many statements, as a rule, whenever the police report a case, in addition to the testimony of the detectives and the statements of the Municipal Council's lawyers, other evidence must be collected to form a conviction, not just relying on the words of the police. This case should also be treated as such to show fairness. In short, whether the defendant's arrest is fair or not is not being discussed here. Now, after two trials, a journalist has been held in custody for such a long time. The lawyer has already stated all the laws that can be cited. The Presiding Judge should pay attention." James Kee-Ong, the legal counsel of the Headquarters, continued to argue, saying that the Municipal Council's lawyer's statement was nothing more than two points: (1) The case should not be under the jurisdiction of the Headquarters; (2) The accusation against the defendant. However, the Army, Navy, and Air Force Trial Regulations he cited did not pay attention to the martial law area at all. The defendant committed the crime in the martial law zone of Jiangsu Province, and the arrest occurred during the period of martial law, so it is of course under the jurisdiction of the Headquarters. Moreover, the National Government recently had a secret order on August 1 that all important Communist cases should be handled by military organs, and even those already accepted by ordinary courts should be transferred to military organs. Although the defendant is not a soldier, the Headquarters absolutely has the right to hear the case. As for the name of the crime, since he is a Communist, he must be interrogated according to the Anti-Revolutionary Punishment Law before a judgment can be made. What should be studied today is the procedure for transfer. Whether or not the crime has been committed will be investigated by the Headquarters. If the interrogation shows that he is innocent, he will not be punished. To conclude that he had not committed a crime before, simply because no anti-revolutionary evidence was found in his residence, is not a solid argument. It is difficult to guarantee that the evidence was not destroyed after the defendant's arrest. It is appropriate to approve the transfer of the case to the Headquarters for trial. The police lawyer further argued against the points of martial law and secret orders, saying that the concession does not belong to the martial law area, and the secret order is not a promulgated law. According to Article 2 of the agreement, any laws and regulations that must be promulgated are effective in this court. The agreement was signed with various countries and is no different from the Constitution of this court, which cannot be changed arbitrarily. Lawyer James immediately retorted, saying that the concession does not belong to the martial law area is a matter of fact, but a notice stating that Shanghai is not in Jiangsu should not be requested. Pudong is in the martial law area of Jiangsu, which should be noted. Lawyer Song slightly argued for the defendant. The defendant requested the court to allow him to confess. The main points were approximately: (1) He resolutely denied the name Hu Yu, saying that investigations could be carried out in all directions; (2) The current event was a blackmail attempt by a Xu surnamed person who was unsuccessful in extorting 50 yuan and fabricated accusations; (3) He cited the cases of lawyer Shen Xingxia and others who were previously falsely accused of being reactionaries as examples and requested to refute the transfer; (4) He applied for bail. Finally, Prosecutor Xu expressed his opinion that the defendant's name had not yet been determined and should be investigated further. Judge Xu then ordered the defendant to be returned to custody and instructed the Headquarters to submit evidence, and rescheduled the trial.

Opening of Trial for Parricide Case 191

Defendants Initially Retract Confessions

Truth Uncovered Through Repeated Interrogation

Sun Laowu, a native of Nantong residing in Qujia Bridge, Zhabei, was brutally murdered at his home on July 27th of this year (corresponding to June 2nd of the leap month in the old calendar) at 7 PM. The crime was perpetrated by his adopted son, Sun Liansheng, along with fellow villagers Ji Shuangquan, Qiu Lansheng, and Qiu Shuntao. Following the act, Sun Liansheng and Qiu Shuntao fled to Nantong but were apprehended by Sun Xuewen (biological father), and Sun Xue Li, among others, who then handed them over to Shanghai authorities. The Fifth Precinct of the Municipal Police Bureau apprehended all the principal offenders. After initial interrogation, all confessed fully. Subsequently, they were transferred to the local court where Prosecutor Xu completed the investigation and filed a public indictment for premeditated murder. Yesterday at 10 AM, Criminal Court President Shen Bingrong commenced the trial. The defendants unexpectedly retracted their confessions and pleaded not guilty. The presiding judge summoned witnesses to the court for cross-examination, and Sun Liansheng was subjected to repeated questioning. Ultimately, he confessed to the premeditated nature of the murder. The trial concluded at 2 PM. Due to the summer recess and the lack of a midday meal, the presiding judge provided the defendants with refreshments. As the detention center's lunch hour had passed, the trial was adjourned for further debate and sentencing. The success in solving the case exemplifies the saying, "The net of Heaven is vast, with sparse meshes, yet nothing escapes it." The testimonies of the defendants and more than ten witnesses are recorded below.

Sun Liansheng:

Official Inquiry: Sun Liansheng testifies, 25 years old, native of Nantong. Sun Laowu is my uncle. I was adopted as his son. Because Ji Shuangquan on June 29th wanted to borrow 50 yuan from my uncle without success. On the afternoon of the second day of the leap month at 8 p.m., he came to borrow money again. My uncle was sleeping in bed. Qiu Lansheng and Qiu Shuntao twisted me outside. Ji Shuangquan killed my uncle. Also Gu Junchuan and Wei Qiaohai were inside.

(Question:) You never said there were these two people inside before.

(Answer:) Ji Shuangquan told me not to betray him.

(Question:) Did you do it?

(Answer:) I was watching them outside. If I had reported it, they would have killed me first.

(Question:) Since you didn't do it, why did you run back to Tongzhou with Qiu Shuntao?

(Answer:) After they killed, they feared I would report it, so they took me back to Nantong to prevent me from reporting.

(Question:) After you arrived in Nantong, you clearly stated to your biological father Sun Xuewen and uncle Sun Xueli that you personally participated, gathered Ji Shuangquan, and Ji asked Qiu Shuntao, Qiu Lansheng, to commit the crime together, and in the police station you confessed that Ji Shuangquan stabbed your uncle's neck with scissors first.

(Answer:) It was under torture.

(Question:) When did you leave for Nantong?

(Answer:) At 9 PM on the second night, Ji Shuangquan forced me to leave.

(Question:) You said the police station tortured you, but why did you speak so clearly to Sun Xuewen? You two fled to Nantong, and Sun Fusheng telegraphed in advance. You were caught at the dock, so later you told your family that you were chasing back the rickshaw that had been sold, so you conspired with Ji Shuangquan, etc., Qiu Shuntao dragged your uncle off the bed, Ji Shuangquan slashed with a knife first, and you stabbed his neck with scissors, Qiu Lansheng hit his face with a hoe, and Qiu Shuntao stabbed again with a shovel. All four did it.

(Answer:) Only they, Ji Shuangquan, Wei Qiaohai, and Gu Junchuan, did it.

(Question:) Who did it first?

(Answer:) Ji Shuangquan.

(Question:) What weapon was used?

(Answer:) Scissors, Gu Junchuan used a hoe, Wei Qiaohai used a shovel.

(Question:) Did Qiu Shuntao and Qiu Lansheng do it outside?

(Answer:) Qiu Lansheng did it, with a kitchen knife.

(Question:) Where did he stab?

(Answer:) On the face.

(Question:) What about Qiu Shuntao?

(Answer:) Watching my actions, I really didn't do it.

(Question:) Stabbing on the bed or stabbing on the ground?

(Answer:) Ji Shuangquan knelt on my uncle, Wei Qiaohai stabbed with scissors, and suddenly said Wei Qiaohai knelt on the deceased and Ji Shuangquan stabbed with a knife.

(Question:) Where did the three weapons of kitchen knife, scissors, and hoe come from?

(Answer:) The shovel is his own, the rest were brought.

(Question:) Are you married?

(Answer:) Yes, I lived in Shanghai for two or three years and returned in the middle of June.

(Question:) Did your uncle have adultery with your wife?

(Answer:) No.

(Question:) Qiu Lansheng once confessed that your wife had adultery with your uncle, you couldn't bear it, so you killed your uncle.

(Answer:) There is no such thing.

Ji Shuangquan:

Official Inquiry: Ji Shuangquan testifies, 30 years old, native of Tongzhou, rickshaw puller. I know Sun Liansheng and Sun Laowu.

(Question:) Why did Sun Liansheng plot to kill his uncle?

(Answer:) I don't know.

(Question:) Did he discuss it with you in advance?

(Answer:) No.

(Question:) You once confessed that Sun Liansheng discussed it with you in advance.

(Answer:) I didn't say that.

(Question:) Sun Liansheng said you were the first to act.

(Answer:) No.

(Question:) Do you know Wu Xiqi?

(Answer:) I know him.

(Question:) Do you live in his house?

(Answer:) It was raining on the second night, I went alone.

(Question:) Why did you go to his house?

(Answer:) Because I couldn't find a house, I stayed for one night.

(Question:) Do you know Qiu Lansheng and Qiu Shuntao?

(Answer:) I know them.

(Question:) Qiu Lansheng said that on the second night you called him to do it and killed Sun Laowu together.

(Answer:) No such thing.

(Question:) Who killed him?

(Answer:) I don't know.

Qiu Lansheng:

Official Inquiry: Qiu Lansheng testifies, 24 years old, native of Tongzhou, farmer. I know Sun Liansheng, Ji Shuangquan is my tenant.

(Question:) When did Ji Shuangquan come to call you?

(Answer:) He didn't come to call me. He moved out on the first day. After Sun Laowu died on the second day, Sun Liansheng came on the third day and said, Ji Shuangquan is my tenant, telling me to hand him over. I asked carpenter Jiang and Zhao Songchun to help find Ji Shuangquan, but on the second day, because I was sick, I didn't go out. I ate snails with Chen Shuda and Zhao Songchun at home.

(Question:) Eating snails only takes a moment. You could also eat after killing someone. When did you eat the snails?

(Answer:) Around 7 o'clock.

(Question:) Where did you buy them?

(Answer:) I found them in the ditch.

(Question:) Who found them?

(Answer:) Ji Shuangquan found them and sent me a total of two catties.

(Question:) This sending of snails is a gift to you, asking you to go to kill someone, to sweeten your mouth, otherwise he would have moved out, would he still send you snails? Besides, you are sick, eating snails will make you bloated. I know you fell for the snail trick, momentarily ate emotionally and killed someone.

The defendant listened and cried non-stop.

Qiu Shuntao:

Official Inquiry: Qiu Shuntao testifies, 28 years old, native of Nantong, road worker, same profession, Qiu Lansheng is the same surname but not from the same clan. I know Sun Liansheng and Ji Shuangquan. On the afternoon of June 2nd at 4 p.m., I met Sun Liansheng in Jiangwan. Everyone wanted to go to Jiangbei, so we went together. We met Wei Qiaohai and Gu Junchuan. They called a rickshaw and sent us to Tiantong Temple, then to the shooting range, took a tram to the 16th Pier, and took a boat to Nantong. We rested in Sun Liansheng's cousin's car dealership. At that time it was the morning of the third day at 10 a.m. Unexpectedly, a telegram from Shanghai arrived in Tong, so Sun Liansheng's father was called to the car dealership, saying that we were murderers and really wronged. If I had killed someone, please shoot me first and then behead me.

(Question:) Where do Gu Junchuan and others live?

(Answer:) In front of Fudan University.

(Question:) Sun Liansheng killed his adoptive father at 7 PM, how could he leave with you at 4 PM?

Also (Question:) What boat did you take?

(Answer:) It was a boat to Tianshenggang, I don't know the name. (To be continued)

Mother Beats Son Case 192

Three-Year-Old Child Dies from Severe Injuries

Chen Yinbao Denies Needle Pricks

Further Interrogation and Examination to Follow Autopsy

Yesterday morning, the Jing'an Temple Police Station dispatched Constable Yang Zaishan to escort 26-year-old Suzhou woman Chen Yinbao to the Special District Court's Criminal Court Two, presided over by Judge Sun Yuan for questioning. Police Attorney Wang Yaotang stated that the Police Station is charging the defendant with severely beating her three-year-old son, Zhou Jishun, between the 28th and 30th of last month at 1192 Hart Road, resulting in his death. The child's body has not yet been transported to the mortuary for autopsy, therefore a request is made for adjournment and further questioning. Zhou Xinfa submitted a deposition, stating that he is a native of Chuansha, Pudong, earning a living by running a small shop. The defendant, Chen Yinbao, is his wife, married for five years, cohabiting at 1192 Hart Road. They have two sons, the elder died of illness at the age of three, the younger is currently three years old, namely Jishun. He has been subjected to beatings by the defendant, leaving his body covered in bruises. On the 25th of last month, he (Zhou) returned home ill and bedridden. The defendant then punched and kicked Jishun, for five consecutive days, also using thread needles to prick Jishun's abdomen, causing severe injuries. He witnessed the heartbreaking events, but due to being afflicted by illness, was unable to stop her, and could only order his apprentice to send Jishun to Baolong Hospital for medical treatment. Doctors attempted to remove the needles. Subsequently, his mother, out of love for her grandson, took Jishun out of the hospital and brought him to Chuansha for further medical treatment. Eventually, due to severe injuries, he died within a few days. Upon hearing the news, he was enraged and reported it to the police, who dispatched detectives to arrest the defendant. Judge Sun asked Zhou where the child's body was located, and whether an examination had been conducted. Zhou replied that the body was in his hometown and had not been examined. Zhou Xinfa's mother, Zhou Wangshi, aged 60, also stated that she resided in Chuansha. After the defendant severely beat her grandson, her son sent apprentice Fu Jizu to send a letter to the village. She rushed to Baolong Hospital in Shanghai and witnessed doctors removing iron needles from her grandson's abdomen. When questioned, defendant Chen Yinbao stated that she lightly disciplined her son because he bit her while she was sleeping, but did not prick his abdomen with a thread needle. Furthermore, Jishun was her own son, and she would not bear to commit such an atrocity. After reviewing the statements, Judge Sun ordered the defendant remanded in custody, and ordered Zhou Xinfa to transport the child's body to the mortuary on Fielun Road for examination.

Zhabei Fu'anli Water Supply Negotiations 195

Public Utilities Bureau Urges Installation of Public Tap

The houses in Fu'anli, Changan Road, Zhabei, originally used tap water, but the water was cut off due to a rent increase issue. The tenants are willing to draw river water and do not want to increase their burden. Last October, the owner, Qu Genji, took over the property. At that time, he originally planned to increase the rent and restore the water supply, but the tenants refused and demanded a rent reduction. Therefore, the water supply problem in the neighborhood has not been resolved. Recently, some tenants sent a letter to the Municipal Public Utilities Bureau, stating that the lack of drinking water is detrimental to hygiene, and is especially dangerous in the event of a fire, requesting assistance. The bureau summoned the owner's representative and the rental accountant to inquire about the situation. After consideration, it was deemed reasonable that the owner was not responsible for the water supply, but it was inappropriate for the tenants to draw river water. Therefore, the Zhabei Water and Electricity Company was ordered to set up a public tap in the neighborhood, and to charge according to the vegetable stall water usage fee regulations recently approved by the municipal government for domestic water companies (i.e., 4 copper coins per bucket of water delivered to each household, 2 copper coins for half a bucket, and 1 copper coin reduction per bucket for those who fetch it themselves. Users can voluntarily pay monthly based on daily water consumption. Retail beverages are also available to provide relief.

Second First Trademark Competition of Shishi News 201

People's hearts are different, just like their faces. Trademarks are the same. The same trademark, square, round, oblique, and neat, has completely different meanings. Try to add comments, and the interest is full. The newspaper previously created the trademark competition on June 6th, and thousands of people participated. Now, all parties are requesting one after another, and it is inevitable to repeat it on the 22nd of this month (i.e., today). All readers of the newspaper can participate. As long as the one you choose is the one you like, you have the hope of winning a prize of 100 yuan. The "Reader Participation Rules" are recorded below: (1) The purpose is to promote commercial credit, encourage the use of trademarks, and hold competitions so that the public has the opportunity to have a common understanding. (2) Voting for the trademark in this session will be printed three times. Readers are free to choose the trademark they think is the most exquisite and vote according to the following methods. (3) Methods (A) Voters must cut and fill in the competition ticket and add a seal, otherwise it will be invalid. (B) Voters must explain the reasons for their approval of the trademark. (C) The statement of reasons must be written in regular script on plain paper, limited to fifty characters. (D) Voters must write "Trademark Competition of Shishi News, Wangping Street, Shanghai" on the cover. (4) Deadline The deadline for voting is from the date of the first publication to the fourteenth day after the third publication. Tickets submitted after the deadline will be invalid. (5) Judges This session will hire Pan Gongzhan, Zhao Jinqing, Yuan Ludeng, Liu Zhanen, and Lin Zhenbin as judges. (6) Awards The reasons submitted by the readers will be publicly judged by the judges. The first five names will be selected based on their accurate wording and neat handwriting. The first place will be rewarded with 100 yuan in cash, and the other four will each receive 10 yuan. Ten days after the competition ends, the winning list will be announced in the newspaper. The winners must prepare the seal used when voting to collect the reward.

Extortion and Assault Case by Hoodlums 206

Trial Held Yesterday

Last month, near the Zhangjia Bridge by the Fenshui Temple in Zhabei, the Chengfa Niupi Factory was targeted by Jiangbei hoodlums for extortion. When they failed, these ruffians gathered over a hundred people and stormed the factory. They tied up the manager, a Cantonese named Dai Ying, and the workers (sixteen people were tied up on the spot), beat them, and completely destroyed the doors, windows, and miscellaneous items of the Chengfa and Tongliyuan (located very close to Chengfa) Niupi Factories. The factory reported this to the local police station, which immediately dispatched officers to the scene. They arrested seven ringleaders: Hong Yikuan, Dai Zhongfu, Liu Yongfu, Chen Wanyu, Sun Zitian, Cai Busheng, and Zhu Changshun. They were taken to the local court prosecutor's office for interrogation, where they confessed to the facts. The defendants were all ordered to be detained. Sun Zitian was released on bail. A lawsuit was filed with the criminal court, requesting a public trial. The main points of the indictment were as follows: the defendants Hong Yikuan, Dai Zhongfu, Liu Yongfu, etc., were all hoodlums who relied on their large gang to extort various leather factories in Zhangjia Bridge. Because the area was remote, no one dared to challenge them. Previously, they had extorted three yuan from Chengfa Factory. Not long after, they demanded another ten yuan. When the factory manager, Dai Ying, refused, they attempted to take the factory's leather as compensation, leading to a conflict. The gang then gathered over a hundred people and stormed the factory, engaging in violent assaults and destroying many doors, windows, and miscellaneous items. The injuries sustained by both sides were not reported. The indictment focused on the Chengfa Factory's charges of extortion, disruption of order, and property damage. Yesterday at 11:00 AM, Judge Zhao opened the trial. The plaintiffs were represented by lawyers Sha Xunyi and Chao Kun, who presented their case. After the judge took his seat, he ordered the detained Hong Yikuan to be brought to the stand. He was 26 years old, from Funing, and worked as a rust scraper on ships. Dai Zhongfu testified that he was 24 years old, from Xinghua, and a laborer. Liu Yongfu testified that he was 27 years old, from Huaicheng, and sold flatbreads. Chen Wanyu testified that he was 42 years old, from Huaicheng, and worked as a rickshaw puller. Sun Zitian testified that he was 26 years old, from Funing. Cai Busheng testified that he was 24 years old, from Yancheng. The testimonies of these individuals were mutually contradictory. Zhu Changshun testified that he was 23 years old, from Yancheng, and was currently recruiting soldiers at the North Railway Station. He presented a triangular recruiting flag made of white bamboo cloth, along with symbols. The judge asked him which army unit he was recruiting for. Zhu replied that it was the First Division of the Army Training Regiment. The judge asked where the division headquarters was stationed. Zhu replied that it was currently at the front lines and claimed to have previously served in the military, now on a long leave to visit family. The judge asked where he had served in the military. Zhu replied that it was the Third Battalion, Eighteenth Regiment, Third Division of the Hunan Army. The judge asked who had ordered him to recruit soldiers. Zhu replied that it was Deputy Officer Wang, also known as Battalion Commander Wang. The judge asked where Wang lived. Zhu replied that Wang lived in the alley behind the Jiaotong Hotel at the Hanqiao Bridge at the North Railway Station. The judge asked how much he was paid each month for recruiting soldiers. Zhu replied twelve yuan. The judge asked if he was impersonating soldiers. Zhu replied that he was not. The judge asked when he started recruiting soldiers. Zhu replied in August of this year. The judge pointed out that he had been in custody since August, so how could he be recruiting in August? Zhu was speechless. The judge ordered the items to be kept on file to be investigated further. Then, the judge ordered the plaintiff, Dai Ying, to the stand. He was 54 years old, from Nanhai, Guangdong, and was the manager of the leather factory. He testified that they (referring to Hong Yikuan, Dai Zhongfu, and Liu Yongfu) had repeatedly extorted two yuan, three yuan, and seven yuan from the factory. This time, they demanded another ten yuan, which he refused. They then gathered over a hundred people and stormed the factory, tying up and assaulting him and the workers, and destroying the doors, windows, and miscellaneous items. At the time, their numbers were so great that they surrounded both factories. The judge asked how many people were in the two factories. Dai replied that the two factories had only thirty-two workers, including children. Witnesses Guo Youcheng, Hu Dayin, and Zhou Guangfa testified that the gang had surrounded the factory and destroyed the doors and windows. After this testimony, the judge invited Prosecutor Zhao Zhiqiu to present his arguments. Sun Zitian's lawyer then stood up to defend Sun, requesting that he be declared innocent. The plaintiffs' lawyers, Sha Xunyi and Chao Kun, spoke in turn. The plaintiff pointed out in court that Chen Wanyu had tied him up at the time, and that Sun Zitian had tied up the workers. The judge then announced that the arguments in the case were concluded and that a verdict would be announced later. The defendants were returned to custody, and Sun Zitian remained on bail pending further notice. The court adjourned.

Apprentice Electrocuted to Death 207

Accidental Step on Live Wire with Bare Feet

Weng Tingfang, an apprentice at the Wenhua Library and Printing House at 150 Zhoujiazu Road, Hongkou, was only seventeen years old and from Ningbo. Yesterday at 2:30 PM, after stopping work, he was going upstairs to rest. Passing through the accounting room, there was an electric fan on the table, with the wire fallen to the ground. Weng accidentally stepped on the wire with his bare feet and immediately fell to the ground and died. At about 3:00 PM, he was sent to Tongren Hospital and then transferred to the forensic examination office on Feilun Road for examination.

Abusing His Son from a Previous Marriage 208

How Can Yuan Zhensheng Be So Heartless?

Yuan Zhensheng, who lives at 128 Kenenghai Road in the Public Concession and works at the tram company, had a son named Jinzhong, now seven years old, from his deceased first wife. Two years ago, Zhensheng remarried a woman named Zhou as his second wife, who gave birth to another son, whom they doted on. As a result, Zhensheng discriminated against his son from his first marriage. Incited by Zhou, Jinzhong was often beaten by his father. Neighbors often heard his cries of pain and were indignant. Yesterday, Zhensheng returned home from the company, and Zhou told him that Jinzhong had secretly taken money and spent it outside. Zhensheng, without investigating whether it was true, immediately beat Jinzhong severely and then burned his neck with a cigarette, causing him to fall to the ground in extreme pain and cry miserably. Neighbors, hearing the sound, went to see what had happened and all felt that Zhensheng was deliberately mistreating his son from his first marriage, showing extreme cruelty. They immediately reported the matter to the Huisi police station, bringing Zhensheng, Zhou, and Jinzhong for investigation. The neighbors were willing to testify. The police chief, after learning the details, found that Zhensheng's abuse of his son from his first marriage was indeed wrong. However, Jinzhong was still young and unable to support himself. Zhensheng and his wife Zhou were reprimanded and ordered to take the child back and raise him properly, with a warning that any further abuse would be severely punished.

Assault Due to Unsuccessful Loan 209

Madam Du Zhang Severely Injured

Du Panlin, from Shaoxing, is currently 41 years old and works as a shop assistant at the Renhe Yuan Soy Sauce Shop near the Lao Zha Bridge. He married Zhang, also 41 years old, when he was young. They live in a flat on the upper floor of a building at a certain number in the Xu Family Garden in the Tangjia Alley nearby. An old Jiangbei man named Lao Chong Bobo lives in the kitchen. He has no permanent job, so he often faces financial difficulties and borrows money from neighbors. Once he borrows, he never returns it. The day before yesterday, he asked Zhang to borrow four yuan but was refused. He had been cursing for days. Until last night, he was still grumbling downstairs. Zhang could no longer tolerate it and questioned him. Lao Chong Bobo became enraged and used a knife to slash her four times: once on the head, once on the left shoulder, once on the back, and once on the abdomen. The cuts were half an inch deep, and blood flowed profusely. She fell to the ground in extreme pain. The sub-landlord reported the incident to police station 102, and the police arrested the perpetrator and took him to the Huisi police station for handling. The injured woman was taken to Tongren Hospital by ambulance and then transferred to Guangren Hospital for treatment. Her life is in danger.

Thieves Disappear in the French Concession 210

Recently, the French Concession police authorities have been very strict with security within the concession and preventive measures against thieves. Detectives are spread out like stars, and several new teams have been organized, each with specific responsibilities. Furthermore, Mr. Huang Jinrong, a senior consultant, has recruited several hundred special volunteers to patrol various locations. This has made it impossible for petty thieves to succeed. As a result, robbery cases have been rare in the past two months.

Lost Girl Awaiting Collection 211

The third district police station reported that on the afternoon of the day before yesterday around 1:00 PM, they found a lost girl, one mouth, with a native accent, at the Lujiazui Wharf in Pudong. She claimed her name was Chen A'e, thirteen years old, from Ningbo. Her parents were deceased, and she only had a grandmother. Today, she followed a soy sauce shop apprentice named A'quan on a ferry to Pudong for fun. A'quan disappeared, so she did not know the way and could not return. The child was wearing a short black cotton shirt and striped cloth trousers, with cropped hair. Because the district police could not determine her address, she was kept to wait for her family to claim her.

Lost Woman Awaiting Collection 212

The Municipal Public Security Bureau reported yesterday that the first precinct of the fourth district had sent in a lost woman, Tang Yangshi, one mouth. She stated that she was 25 years old, from Wu County. Her father's name was Yang Yinchu, and he used to run a wild game store in Suzhou, but it has now closed. Her mother, Zhang, lives in Tonghui Road, Zhou Shanbang 35, Wuxi, with the old address being Yuan No. 2. Her husband's name is Tang Hongsheng, and he used to work as a shoemaker in Shanghai, but she doesn't know where he is now. She came to Shanghai to find her husband but was unsuccessful and couldn't find work, so she got lost. The woman has thick eyebrows and a sallow complexion, suggesting she may have a mental illness. She is wearing a blue striped cloth shirt, black gauze trousers, and black cloth shoes. She has been sent to the Xin Puyu Tang to be cared for. A letter has been sent to the Wuxi County Public Security Bureau to inquire about her family and ask them to come to Shanghai to claim her.

The matter concerns the bond for the disarmament funds raised by this office. From late September of last year to February 14 of this year, which falls under the supervisory period, the funds raised by various customs branches, except for the losses during the political changes from December 6 of last year to January 23 of this year, should be handled by former Supervisor He to ensure the integrity of the debt. The funds raised in the other months were all reported and officially redeemed by former Supervisor He, and then redistributed. Since February 15 of this year, after this customs office was placed under the jurisdiction of the Inspector General of Customs, up to the end of March when the fundraising stopped, which is 45 days, the total amount of funds raised by former Customs Commissioner He and this customs office was 22,931 yuan, which has been fully submitted. We have now received the official disarmament bonds and need to redistribute them separately. As for the due principal and interest, and the standard 98% discount, this office has prepared a payment schedule, with one attached to each bond for the bondholder to check and receive the principal and interest. In addition to instructing various customs branches to collect and redistribute them quickly, and to inform all merchants and citizens, we are writing to your association to request that you inform all merchants and citizens that if they hold disarmament bond receipts issued after February 15 of this year, they should immediately collect them in increments of ten yuan and exchange them for official bonds at the original fundraising customs branches. As for the interest due and the return of the two-point discount, this office has calculated the amounts and prepared a list, with one attached to each bond. The bondholder should sign and stamp the list and receive the full amount from the original fundraising customs branches. In addition to instructing various customs branches to issue and exchange the bonds immediately upon request, without any delay or extortion, all merchants and citizens should not delay and cause inconvenience. This is very important. We are forwarding this letter and request that you check it and notify your colleagues. If you hold disarmament bond receipts issued by this customs office after February 15 of this year, please collect them in increments of ten yuan and exchange them for official bonds at the original fundraising customs branches and collect the due interest and two-point discount. This is very important. We are sending this letter and request that you check it. If you hold this bond receipt, please follow the procedure and exchange it for an official bond at the original fundraising customs branch. This is for the attention of all major pharmacies. Issued by the Shanghai New Drug Trade Association."

Letter to the Editor 214

Greetings, I have just read the article "Recent Events at the China Merchants Bureau - Continued Operation of the Navigation School" in today's news section of your newspaper. It states that "the teaching staff of the navigation specialty first sent representatives to meet with Cai, requesting that the status quo be maintained, and that Cai immediately presented it to the Ministry of Communications, stating that the teachers and students of the school had come to the Bureau to request that the merger be avoided," etc. After reading this, I was very surprised. After the teaching staff of the navigation specialty received the official letter from Acting Principal Cai regarding the merger of this school with the Wusong Merchant Marine School, they immediately followed the instructions in the letter and completed all handover procedures for the school's affairs in preparation for the transfer. However, because the staff had not been paid their salaries for the four months from May to August, and repeated requests for payment had been unsuccessful, they were forced to send several representatives to meet with Acting Principal Cai on the 18th and 19th of this month to demand payment of their salaries so that they could prepare to return home. Regarding the school's affairs, they immediately stated that they had completed the handover according to the letter and were waiting for the transfer. There was no request to maintain the status quo or any other negotiations. This is the true situation of the meeting with Acting Principal Cai on that day. As for the students' movement to protect the school, the declaration issued, and the negotiations with Acting Principal Cai, it was entirely the action of the entire student body, and the staff did not participate in any of it. The information in your newspaper is likely due to incorrect rumors. We are sending this letter to request a correction and to have our letter published to avoid misunderstandings. With best wishes, the entire teaching staff of the China Merchants School Navigation Specialty, August 21.

To the Editor-in-Chief of Shen Bao, I have just read the section in your newspaper today regarding the case of Deng Zhulan from Pingyang and her brother-in-law, Wen Ming, being accused of abduction by her cousin, Deng Jing. It states that "after the woman came to Shanghai, she was admitted to Datong University," etc. After checking, our school has no such person as Deng Zhulan among the newly admitted students this time. The information in your newspaper is not consistent with the facts. We are sending this letter to request a correction. Best wishes, Datong University, August 20. Sincerely, I have just read the local news section of your newspaper, which stated that "our association is a disguised lottery and was searched by the French police," etc., which is not consistent with the facts. Our association opened at the beginning of this month and was registered with the French Consulate in Shanghai. We have raised 100,000 yuan in capital and aim to promote savings. To generate interest, we hold periodic draws. Although we were mistakenly searched by the French police yesterday, the items have been returned in full today, and we are operating as usual. We are concerned that this may cause misunderstandings, and we request that you correct the information. To the Editor-in-Chief of Shen Bao, Yongnian Savings Association, August 21.

Art World

Black Drama 216

— Yang Changxi

Besides music, the art form that best expresses the strong national consciousness of black people is painting and drama.

In painting, they do not yet have independent ability, because painting is an aristocratic pursuit. It cannot be successful without sufficient economic resources and ample time for practice. Therefore, even if they achieve something, they cannot escape the influence of white people.

Apart from the occasional exhibition of works by black people who have resided in France in the past, in the United States there are a few young writers who have been fostered by grants and awards from a certain society. However, their expressive power in painting is fundamentally weak. Apart from taking the lives of wandering black people or street performers as themes to express black life, there is no other mature national consciousness in painting than in literature.

In drama, because their skills in creating scripts are relatively weak, their achievements in acting outweigh the work of playwrights. Therefore, there are black members in all kinds of theater troupes in the United States. On the one hand, they have a talent for acting; on the other hand, to express the life and suffering of modern black people, it is impossible without them. Therefore, many themes in American dramas use black people as the background, because black people cannot be separated from real life in the United States, and the lower-class life of black people is a member of the flourishing American civilization.

The most famous actor and director is Paul Robeson. He is not only the first outstanding talent among black people, but also a well-known figure in contemporary American theater history. The most famous is his staging of the play "Othello." After its success in England and Paris, his position in the United States has increased. He is only a 35-year-old young man. His unique success is especially due to his singing and expressions that contain the spirit of the Negro race. Because he is a lucky man of the times, he became famous for acting in two plays by the American playwright Eugene O'Neill. He studied at Latin Kings University, so his acting skills can sharply express the talent of black people.

In addition, the film industry, which has been popular in the United States in recent years and has almost conquered the world, cannot escape the influence of black people. In addition to adopting black people in the themes and actors, they also have organizations that are completely directed and played by black people. King Vidor, the creator of the most famous "The Big Parade," caused a stir in the United States and Germany with his film "Hallelujah," starring only black people. In order to completely and realistically depict the lives of black people in "Hallelujah," Vidor personally went to the black areas of the southern United States to select excellent actors. All the faces, postures, songs and dances, and the consciousness of the masses can fully express the entire life of the black people. Therefore, in the three major elements of American civilization, music ("Gazz"), black people have injected the blood of their nation, making American national music completely black. Although black people cannot conquer the film that represents modern American civilization, the style of film cannot escape the black background.

In the production of scripts, due to the times, their success is not as great as in novels and poetry. Most of them are simple descriptions of the lives of black people. Moreover, because there are many abbreviations and dialects in the unique English of black people, as well as the infiltration of foreign languages, it is difficult to gain the sympathy and understanding of non-black audiences in the performance. Only by staging them in theaters unique to black people can the themes be used as tools to awaken national consciousness.

However, in the development process of black drama, the most noteworthy are Jonathan Matheus, who won the "Opportunity Magazine" drama award in 1926 with the one-act play "The Recruiters," and Ceorgia Douglas Johnson, who won the first place in the magazine's drama competition in 1927 with "Plumes."

In "Plumes," he very deeply portrays the tragedy of a woman who gets sick. It is a personal tragedy, not about black people, but the short one-act play is full of emotions that make people have to sympathize.

But "The Recruiters" is different. Although it is also a short one-act play, it can deeply express that after Lincoln freed the slaves, their lives were still subject to disguised slavery. A typical 73-year-old nanny grandmother can only sing when life is not good, "No one knows the hardships I have encountered, only Jesus knows..." And the grandson, a 23-year-old Negro youth, has to admit the needs of the recruiters of the Northern Arsenal for the sake of life, because the white recruiter said to the young man, "Don't lose the good opportunity of your life, there is good money and a good career waiting for you." And he can make his grandmother's life stable and his wife beautiful, so he has to admit it.

In short, the expression of national consciousness in black art is becoming sharper day by day. To restore their Greater Afro-America, it is necessary to have the stimulant of national character in art.

Commemorating the Poet Huang Zhenxia 217

— Qiuyuan

The day before yesterday, my brother Fu Yanchang casually reported to me that he didn't know the whereabouts of Huang Zhenxia and said that Huang Zhenxia had gone to the front, and his life and death were uncertain. Those who have even a slight acquaintance with this unfortunate poet Huang Zhenxia will inevitably express infinite sympathy and think of the sadness of life being like a sojourn and fate being difficult to disobey. Yesterday, my brother Lu Mengshu came to my house and talked about Huang Zhenxia. We couldn't help but feel sad for each other. Huang Zhenxia, where is Huang Zhenxia?

Today is Sunday. The first page of the "Shenbao Pictorial Weekly" attached to the Shenbao publishes a photograph of "The Second Cavalry Division of the Central Teaching Corps waiting at Pukou Railway Station on August 1st to go to the front line." From that blurry and dim photograph, we see a young man in military uniform riding a horse, his thin figure, and delicate face. Could it be our poet Huang Zhenxia's last image?

This kind of, that kind of, vague and sorrowful emotion makes us feel the changes of life and the dangers of fate. We commemorate our poet Huang Zhenxia today, even though it may be a bit early. Even though Huang Zhenxia may not have encountered the situation we imagined, this little bit of unfortunate news is enough to make us feel something in our hearts.

…………………………

The readers of this journal may not have forgotten our poet, Huang Zhenxia. In the past, this journal published many of his articles on art history and culture. His powerful writing, vigorous thinking, and beautiful words may still be in the memory of the general readers. Today, what we commemorate is precisely this our poet, this close friend of our journal, Huang Zhenxia.

…………………………

This was three years ago. In an autumn, on North Sichuan Road, known as "Mysterious Street," in the Cantonese Nan Restaurant, in a small room, filled with more than a dozen people, here, I first met our poet, his delicate face, thin figure, crisp Beijing accent, gentle demeanor, at a glance, you could tell he was from a prominent family. He was the youngest and most silent in the group.

He was a student of history, a student of art, and also, he was a poet.

The unfortunate event began like this: his mother passed away from appendicitis two years ago, leaving behind our poet and his sister. The hustle and bustle of the metropolis made lonely people feel even lonelier, and wandering people feel even more adrift. At this time, we saw his poems and articles in various publications such as "Art World" and "Athens."

In the Athens Monthly, Huang Zhenxia published many new poems. His poems have a magnificent, heroic, and unrestrained spirit—in our new poetry world, he can be regarded as unique and unparalleled. From these, those, the poems he left behind, it is already a fact that Huang Zhenxia is our poet, his poems are as majestic as Byron's, but the position he has achieved in the Chinese poetry world—is only our poet, our Byron. The poet's achievements, where has there ever been genius? Fate is truly in control.

Huang Zhenxia was also a nationalist. The essays on art published in "Art World" are full of rich and sound national thought. He was a pioneer of nationalist literature and art. He not only published essays on national literature and art, but also was a creator and practitioner of national literature and art. Many of the poems and novels he left behind are not only full of magnificent and unrestrained temperament, but also contain a large amount of national color. They are typical representative plays of our nationalist literature and art.

National passion, heroic aspirations, and the sorrow of reality led our poet to join the Central Military Academy. We were hoping that this was the dawn of the beginning of his life. But because of the turmoil in the Central Plains, our poet had to embark on a military vehicle and head to the front. He was in the cavalry, on the battlefield in the Guide area. In the battle of Guide, our poet may be among the many names who died in battle. This is the situation, this may be the end of our poet.

Our poet has an unspeakable wandering life experience. He left behind a younger sister, who is currently being cared for by Mr. Zhang Ruogu. He was most friendly with Zhu Yingpeng, Fu Yanchang, Lu Mengshu, and others. He was a Shanghai native of Guangdong origin, and was twenty-one years old.

Page 19

Guidelines for Youth Garden Contributions 218

(1) The scope of articles should be discussions on youth issues, news about domestic and foreign schools or students, essays, descriptions of school life, etc. The style is not limited.

(2) The scope of books is limited to those concerning youth issues.

(3) Qualified photographs should depict youth life (such as sports, travel, excursions, drama, speeches, gatherings, exhibitions, various competitions, etc.), school news, and youth movements. Individuals and groups are welcome.

(4) Do not write on both sides of the manuscript paper.

(5) The number of words per article should not exceed 2,000.

(6) Do not write manuscripts horizontally, and do not write sloppily. Western languages should be omitted where possible. If it is absolutely necessary to quote the original text, it must be attached below the translation.

(7) Do not use blue ink to draw pictures, and do not use colored paper. White paper and black ink must be used.

(8) Please indicate "Youth Garden Editorial Department" for submissions.

(9) Whether or not contributions are published, they will not be returned. If a return is required, it should be stated in advance and sufficient postage should be attached.

(10) Remuneration for articles is divided into three categories: three yuan, two yuan, and one yuan per thousand words. The same applies to pictures and photographs per piece. If there are special contributions, the remuneration will be calculated separately.

Guidelines for Women's Life Contributions 219

(1) The scope of articles should be discussions on women's issues, news about domestic and foreign women, descriptions of women's lives, essays, etc. The style is not limited.

(2) The scope of drawings is limited to those concerning women's issues.

(3) Qualified photographs should depict women's news, women's issues, and women's lives. Individuals and groups are extremely welcome.

The number of words per article should not exceed 2,000.

(4) Do not write on both sides of the manuscript paper.

(5) The number of words per article should not exceed 2,000.

(6) Do not write manuscripts horizontally, and do not write sloppily. Western languages should be omitted where possible. If it is absolutely necessary to quote the original text, it must be attached below the translation.

(7) Do not use blue ink to draw pictures, and do not use colored paper. White paper and black ink must be used.

(8) Please indicate "Women's Life Editorial Department" for submissions.

(9) Whether or not contributions are published, they will not be returned. If a return is required, it should be stated in advance and sufficient postage should be attached.

(10) Remuneration for articles is divided into three categories: three yuan, two yuan, and one yuan per thousand words. The same applies to pictures and photographs. If there are special contributions, the remuneration will be calculated separately.

Book and Newspaper Introduction

Film 223

— Jia

Edited by Lu Mengshu

Published by Wenhua Fine Arts Publishing and Printing Company

It is really shameful that Chinese people seem to be completely unfamiliar with this art—the emerging art of film—as if there is a thick curtain separating them. Although it is said that China also has so-called domestic films, its history has been around for eighteen years (from 1913 to now). However, China's so-called domestic films are nothing more than "pictures in the painting are real, about to come out" like gourds, printing men and women and scenery on film to add another item to the sales market for imported goods. What is film? They still don't understand at all. Because what they understand, on the viewer's side, is nothing more than "pictures in the painting are really real, about to come out." On the producer's side, it is nothing more than a kind of fresh—fashionable—business product like a revolving lantern, in which there are active forms in the painting, that can coax children and deceive rural people to get big money. What is the central consciousness of film art? In fact, they—viewers and producers—are still at a loss, and still don't understand at all.

Because of this lack of understanding, China's so-called domestic films do not know what they have become, and are terribly deformed. This is not my intention to ridicule the viewers and producers of China's so-called domestic films here. This is really a fact that has been shown to us for more than ten years.

Mr. Lu Mengshu is one of the people who has worked the hardest to attack this point. He showed us very clearly in his past work in the eighteen issues of "Silver Star". Now, he is planning to charge again, and the "Film" monthly magazine, which has determined its purpose with all its strength, has appeared.

We should thank him for supporting him for so diligently connecting a group of writers in this era to make this great contribution within the scope of film, and for providing sincere enlightenment and encouragement to the producers of China's so-called domestic films, especially for the sincerity of his attitude towards the readers of the "Film" monthly magazine.

He said in the editor's afterword in the second issue of "Film" monthly magazine, "When I first set the editorial plan for this magazine, I wanted to make it a complete publication in all aspects. However, now it is impossible. Because, in the current state of wavering thoughts, young people feel at a loss. If a magazine of the times inconsistently publishes contradictory remarks, it will confuse young readers, and then the consequences will be endless, and the editor will be equivalent to the culprit."

He also said, "I plan to publish a "Nationalist Film Movement Special Issue" in the fourth issue of this magazine to call on people to recognize the central consciousness of this emerging art. I think this is what I should do for our nation."

That's right, advocating nationalism is what we should do for our nation. Moreover, in this era of national suffering

Page 24

of the times, in this era of declining literature and art, the advocacy of "nationalism" is the most important and urgent thing we should do for our nation first. Because the current crisis in China is that the people have no national consciousness, and are a pile of loose sand with no whole force of unity. They cannot unite internally, and they cannot resist strong enemies externally. The so-called "people are knives and cutting boards, and I am fish and meat." The people of the whole country, like a pile of loose sand, have no national consciousness, so there is no whole force of unity. Since there is no whole force of unity, our nation and national rights will be like the donkey that Shandong people buy donkey meat from, and people can cut off any piece they want. We Chinese have such a current crisis, and we should responsibly hurry up and work hard for the national purpose, which is "nationalism."

We advocate "nationalism", of course, starting from literature and art, because this can determine the center of thought, this can save the decline of literature and art, and this can make all the people recognize national consciousness and achieve a whole force of unity to achieve the self-determination period. Since film is an emerging art, then "nationalism" should be advocated in a film publication. It is true as Mr. Lu Mengshu said, "This is what I should do for our nation."

Sure enough, Mr. Lu Mengshu really has come to do his will, that is, to "completely overturn the original editorial plan, and summarize it to the unity of thought." That is to say, what he showed us is already in the third issue of the "Film" monthly magazine that he edited. In the third issue of the "Film" monthly magazine, the first arrow was shot at the hearts of the producers, in the "Our Words" talk—

It is not to seek correction from the enlightened, nor to seek appreciation from the intellectual class, but to blow a conch shell in the newspaper when it is released, deceive ignorant women and children, make a noise in the lower class society, make money and then do it again, and then find a way to make money. There must always be a way to think of, and it is okay to continue one after another until more than ten sequels. This is also the usual trick of Chinese filmmakers, and it is also the only way for Chinese films.

Although film is one of the enterprises, it is always art, and it cannot be taken casually to be a cover for cheating money, and it cannot be taken casually to deceive the ignorant and promote corruption. Unfortunately, Chinese filmmakers have committed these two problems...

For more than ten years, the original intention has always remained unchanged, and it has become the declining period of Chinese films today.

Mr. Lu has always been bold in speaking, and in this speech, he is especially stern and upright, and his needles are sharp. However, there is always a reason why Chinese films have declined, so he also said—

"In short, this is entirely because thought has lost its center, and culture has no way out, so that all arts have entered a period of decline..."

Yes, because thought has lost its center and culture has no way out, so that all arts have entered a period of decline, so it is not only film, but other things are also the same. Therefore, "If we writers and artists do not urgently catch up and strive to take on this major responsibility, we will not be able to save this crisis in our lifetime." However, how can this major responsibility be taken on with effort? Oh, Mr. Lu told us in the article "Our Understanding of Film Art"—

Today, in this era of suffering in China, we should abandon ourselves and strive to be soldiers fighting for the whole nation. People's will is to survive. We Chinese should have the will to survive for the whole nation."

The literary and artistic movement of "nationalism" is to take consistent action on different fields to work hard on the work, that is, to gather writers, musicians, and other artists, concentrate their minds, unite their forces, and work hard on the "nationalist literary and artistic movement."

For this, Mr. Lu wanted "our understanding of film art", and this "our understanding of film art" is to demand the new life of our film practitioners today, today's new life is to abandon the previous errors in understanding of film and awaken and have a new and correct understanding. This kind of new and correct understanding is the artistic ideological center of "nationalism".

This third issue of the "Film" monthly magazine is sparing no effort in advocating "nationalism". There are too many things that can be said here. The editor's obvious point of expectation for the compatriots' physique is especially admirable. He said on the second page, "Domestic films, in terms of women, have already made people see success... But the requirements of the times are to be fully possessed of male beauty." And on page 45, he said, "In this period of national revival movement, we must pay special attention to the nation's lively and perseverance spirit, and sound physique, because with these two can we have the power of resistance and all actions, which is an urgent need of the nation."

As for the novelty of the layout of this publication, the excellence of the materials, the beauty of the pictures and photos, and the richness of the fun, I dare say that it is unique in film publications. However, after reading this third issue, I still hope that Mr. Lu will publish the fourth issue "Nationalist Film Movement Special Issue" sooner.

Guidelines for Book and Newspaper Introduction Contributions 224

(1) The scope of articles is limited to introducing the latest publications at home and abroad. In addition to literary and artistic works, all political, economic, legal, scientific, educational, etc. books and newspapers are included in the introduction, but boring books and newspapers will not be introduced.

(2) The scope of drawings is limited to the latest works by new writers at home and abroad and attached illustrations related to the text.

(3) Articles on textual research or research on ancient Chinese books will not be published.
